The model: (1) compute MSTR market cap proxy = MSTR_price * shares_outstanding (or use market cap if available); (2) compute BTC NAV = BTC_holdings * BTC_price; (3) apply discount factor from 10Y yield + 1.8% FX hedge premium; (4) compute NPV of BTC holdings = BTC_NAV / (1 + discount_rate); (5) compute premium/discount % = (MSTR_market_cap - NPV) / NPV * 100. Print all intermediate and final results. (Using builtin:python_interpreter)
